      "Employé 11 : Matin = Réclamation     | Après-midi = Réclamation     | Même ? ✓\n",
      "Employé 12 : Matin = Dérogation      | Après-midi = Dérogation      | Même ? ✓\n",

   "source": [
    "from ortools.sat.python import cp_model\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Paramètres\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "num_employees = 12\n",
    "num_days = 5\n",
    "num_shifts = 2  # 0 = matin, 1 = après-midi\n",
    "activities = [\"Téléphone\", \"Renseignement\", \"Dérogation\", \"Impayés\", \"Réclamation\"]\n",
    "num_activities = len(activities)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes minimales par shift\n",
    "min_staff = {\n",
    "    0: 5,  # Téléphone\n",
    "    1: 3,  # Renseignement\n",
    "    2: 1,  # Dérogation\n",
    "    3: 1,  # Impayés\n",
    "    # 4 (Réclamation) : pas de minimum\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Modèle\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "model = cp_model.CpModel()\n",
    "\n",
    "# Variables : assignment[e][d][s] = activité (entier 0-4)\n",
    "assignment = {}\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        for s in range(num_shifts):\n",
    "            assignment[(e, d, s)] = model.NewIntVar(0, num_activities - 1, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}_s{s}')\n",
    "\n",
    "# Variables booléennes : same_activity[e][d] = 1 si matin == après-midi\n",
    "same_activity = {}\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        same_activity[(e, d)] = model.NewBoolVar(f'same_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        # Contrainte : same_activity ⇔ assignment[e,d,0] == assignment[e,d,1]\n",
    "        model.Add(assignment[(e, d, 0)] == assignment[(e, d, 1)]).OnlyEnforceIf(same_activity[(e, d)])\n",
    "        model.Add(assignment[(e, d, 0)] != assignment[(e, d, 1)]).OnlyEnforceIf(same_activity[(e, d)].Not())\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes de couverture minimale (par jour ET par shift)\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "    for s in range(num_shifts):\n",
    "        # Pour chaque activité avec minimum requis\n",
    "        for a in min_staff:\n",
    "            # Compter combien d'employés font l'activité 'a' ce jour/shift\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'count_b_e{e}_d{d}_s{s}_a{a}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignment[(e, d, s)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignment[(e, d, s)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools) >= min_staff[a])\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Objectif : maximiser le nombre de (employé, jour) avec même activité matin/après-midi\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "total_same = model.NewIntVar(0, num_employees * num_days, 'total_same')\n",
    "model.Add(total_same == sum(same_activity[(e, d)] for e in range(num_employees) for d in range(num_days)))\n",
    "model.Maximize(total_same)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Résolution\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "solver = cp_model.CpSolver()\n",
    "solver.parameters.max_time_in_seconds = 30.0\n",
    "solver.parameters.num_search_workers = 8\n",
    "\n",
    "status = solver.Solve(model)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Affichage\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "if status in (cp_model.FEASIBLE, cp_model.OPTIMAL):\n",
    "    print(\"✅ Planning trouvé !\")\n",
    "    print(f\"Nombre total de (employé, jour) avec même activité matin/après-midi : {solver.Value(total_same)} / {num_employees * num_days}\\n\")\n",
    "    \n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        print(f\"--- Jour {d+1} ---\")\n",
    "        for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "            matin = activities[solver.Value(assignment[(e, d, 0)])]\n",
    "            aprem = activities[solver.Value(assignment[(e, d, 1)])]\n",
    "            meme = \"✓\" if solver.Value(same_activity[(e, d)]) else \"✗\"\n",
    "            print(f\"Employé {e+1:2d} : Matin = {matin:15} | Après-midi = {aprem:15} | Même ? {meme}\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    print(\"❌ Aucun planning ne satisfait les contraintes minimales.\")"
   ]
  },

      "✅ Planning trouvé !\n",
      "Nombre de (employé, jour) avec même activité (et présents les 2 shifts) : 61 / 75\n",
      "\n",
      "     A           B           C           D           E           F           G           H           I           J           K           L           M           N           O\n",
      "Tél   Tél   Rens  Rens    *   Rens  Récla Récla   *   Dérog Rens  Rens  Rens  Rens  Tél   Tél   Rens  Rens  Rens  Rens  Imp   Imp   Tél   Tél   Dérog Dérog Rens  Rens    *     *   \n",
      "Rens  Rens  Rens  Rens  Imp   Imp   Dérog Dérog Tél   Tél   Tél   Tél   Tél   Tél     *   Rens  Tél   Tél   Tél   Tél   Récla Récla Tél   Tél     *   Dérog Tél   Tél     *     *   \n",
      "Tél   Tél   Rens  Rens  Tél   Tél   Tél   Tél   Tél   Tél     *   Rens    *   Dérog Tél   Tél   Rens  Rens  Tél   Tél   Tél   Tél   Récla Récla Dérog Dérog Imp   Imp     *     *   \n",
      "Tél   Tél   Tél   Tél     *   Dérog Tél   Tél     *   Rens  Tél   Tél   Tél   Tél   Imp   Imp     *   Rens  Dérog Dérog Récla Récla Rens  Rens  Rens  Rens  Tél   Tél     *     *   \n",
      "Récla Récla Tél   Tél   Imp   Imp   Tél   Tél   Dérog Dérog Tél   Tél   Tél   Tél   Rens  Rens  Tél   Tél   Dérog Dérog Rens  Rens  Rens  Rens  Rens  Rens  Tél   Tél     *     *   \n",
      "\n"

   "source": [
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "import pandas as pd\n",
    "from ortools.sat.python import cp_model\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Paramètres\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "num_employees = 15\n",
    "num_days = 5\n",
    "num_shifts = 2  # 0 = matin, 1 = après-midi\n",
    "activities = [\"Tél\", \"Rens\", \"Dérog\", \"Récla\", \"Imp\"]#, \"Libre\"]\n",
    "num_activities = len(activities)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes minimales par shift\n",
    "min_staff = {\n",
    "    0: 5,  # Téléphone\n",
    "    1: 2,  # Renseignement\n",
    "    2: 1,  # Dérogation\n",
    "    3: 1,  # Réclamation\n",
    "    4: 1,  # Impayés\n",
    "    # 5: 0,  # Libre\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "max_staff = {\n",
    "    0: 7,  # Pas plus de 7 en Téléphone\n",
    "    1: 5,  # Pas plus de 5 en Renseignement\n",
    "    2: 2,  # Pas plus de 2 en Dérogation\n",
    "    3: 1,  # Pas plus de 2 en Réclamation\n",
    "    4: 1,  # Pas plus de 2 en Impayés\n",
    "    # 5: 1,  # Pas plus de 1 en Libre\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "min_monday_staff = {\n",
    "    0: 3,  # Téléphone\n",
    "    1: 5,  # Renseignement\n",
    "    2: 1,  # Dérogation\n",
    "    3: 1,  # Réclamation\n",
    "    4: 1,  # Impayés\n",
    "    # 5: 0,  # Libre\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "max_monday_staff = {\n",
    "    0: 5,  # Pas plus de 7 en Téléphone\n",
    "    1: 7,  # Pas plus de 5 en Renseignement\n",
    "    2: 2,  # Pas plus de 2 en Dérogation\n",
    "    3: 1,  # Pas plus de 2 en Réclamation\n",
    "    4: 1,  # Pas plus de 2 en Impayés\n",
    "    # 5: 1,  # Pas plus de 1 en Libre\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Congés :\n",
    "# shift: 0 = matin, 1 = après-midi\n",
    "\n",
    "size = 10\n",
    "conges = set(zip(np.random.choice(np.arange(num_employees - 2), size = size).tolist(), \n",
    "                 np.random.choice(np.arange(num_days), size = size).tolist(),\n",
    "                 [0] * size))\n",
    "conges.update({(14, i, 0) for i in range(num_days)})  # Employé 15 absent tous les matins\n",
    "conges.update({(14, i, 1) for i in range(num_days)})  # Employé 15 absent tous les matins\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Modèle\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "model = cp_model.CpModel()\n",
    "\n",
    "# Variables\n",
    "assignment = {}      # activité si présent\n",
    "works = {}           # booléen : travaille ce shift ?\n",
    "is_tel = {}\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        for s in range(num_shifts):\n",
    "            works[(e, d, s)] = model.NewBoolVar(f'works_e{e}_d{d}_s{s}')\n",
    "            assignment[(e, d, s)] = model.NewIntVar(0, num_activities - 1, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}_s{s}')\n",
    "            is_tel[(e, d, s)] = model.NewBoolVar(f'is_tel_e{e}_d{d}_s{s}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignment[(e, d, s)] == 0).OnlyEnforceIf(is_tel[(e, d, s)])\n",
    "            model.Add(assignment[(e, d, s)] != 0).OnlyEnforceIf(is_tel[(e, d, s)].Not())\n",
    "\n",
    "# Congés\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        for s in range(num_shifts):\n",
    "            # Si l'employé est en congé ce shift → works = False\n",
    "            if (e, d, s) in conges:\n",
    "                # print(f\"Employé {e} en congé jour {d} shift {s}\")\n",
    "                model.Add(works[(e, d, s)] == 0)\n",
    "                # model.Add(assignment[(e, d, 1 - s)] > 0)\n",
    "                model.Add(is_tel[(e, d, 1 - s)] == 0)\n",
    "            # Sinon, il peut travailler ou non (optionnel). Si tu veux qu'il travaille toujours sauf congé, décommente :\n",
    "            else:\n",
    "                model.Add(works[(e, d, s)] == 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes de couverture : min ET max par shift\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "    for s in range(num_shifts):\n",
    "        for a in range(num_activities):\n",
    "            # Déterminer min et max pour cette activité\n",
    "            min_req, max_req = 0, num_employees\n",
    "\n",
    "            if d % 5 == 0:  # Lundi\n",
    "                min_req = min_monday_staff.get(a, 0)\n",
    "                max_req = max_monday_staff.get(a, num_employees)\n",
    "            else:\n",
    "                min_req = min_staff.get(a, 0)               # 0 si pas de min\n",
    "                max_req = max_staff.get(a, num_employees)   # pas de max → tout le monde\n",
    "\n",
    "            # Si aucune contrainte, on peut sauter (optionnel)\n",
    "            if min_req == 0 and max_req >= num_employees:\n",
    "                continue\n",
    "\n",
    "            # Compter les employés présents ET affectés à l'activité 'a'\n",
    "            count_vars = []\n",
    "            for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "                is_assigned = model.NewBoolVar(f'is_assigned_e{e}_d{d}_s{s}_a{a}')\n",
    "                # is_assigned = 1 ⇔ (works[e,d,s] == 1 ET assignment[e,d,s] == a)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignment[(e, d, s)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf([works[(e, d, s)], is_assigned])\n",
    "                model.Add(assignment[(e, d, s)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf([works[(e, d, s)], is_assigned.Not()])\n",
    "                model.Add(is_assigned == 0).OnlyEnforceIf(works[(e, d, s)].Not())\n",
    "                count_vars.append(is_assigned)\n",
    "\n",
    "            total_count = sum(count_vars)\n",
    "\n",
    "            # Appliquer min et max\n",
    "            if min_req > 0:\n",
    "                model.Add(total_count >= min_req)\n",
    "            if max_req < num_employees:\n",
    "                model.Add(total_count <= max_req)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Stabilité : même activité si les deux shifts sont travaillés\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "same_activity = {}\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        same_activity[(e, d)] = model.NewBoolVar(f'same_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        # Condition : les deux shifts sont travaillés ET activités égales\n",
    "        both_work = model.NewBoolVar(f'both_work_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        model.AddMinEquality(both_work, [works[(e, d, 0)], works[(e, d, 1)]])\n",
    "\n",
    "        # Si les deux travaillent, alors same_activity ⇔ activités égales\n",
    "        equal_act = model.NewBoolVar(f'equal_act_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        model.Add(assignment[(e, d, 0)] == assignment[(e, d, 1)]).OnlyEnforceIf(equal_act)\n",
    "        model.Add(assignment[(e, d, 0)] != assignment[(e, d, 1)]).OnlyEnforceIf(equal_act.Not())\n",
    "\n",
    "        # same_activity = both_work AND equal_act\n",
    "        model.AddBoolAnd([both_work, equal_act]).OnlyEnforceIf(same_activity[(e, d)])\n",
    "        model.AddBoolOr([both_work.Not(), equal_act.Not()]).OnlyEnforceIf(same_activity[(e, d)].Not())\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Objectif : maximiser la stabilité\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "total_same = model.NewIntVar(0, num_employees * num_days, 'total_same')\n",
    "model.Add(total_same == sum(same_activity.values()))\n",
    "model.Maximize(total_same)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Résolution\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "solver = cp_model.CpSolver()\n",
    "# solver.parameters.max_time_in_seconds = 30.0\n",
    "# solver.parameters.num_search_workers = 8\n",
    "solver.parameters.enumerate_all_solutions = True\n",
    "solution_limit = 10\n",
    "status = solver.Solve(model)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Affichage\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "if status in (cp_model.FEASIBLE, cp_model.OPTIMAL):\n",
    "    print(\"✅ Planning trouvé !\")\n",
    "    print(f\"Nombre de (employé, jour) avec même activité (et présents les 2 shifts) : {solver.Value(total_same)} / {num_employees * num_days}\\n\")    \n",
    "    print(\"     \" + \"           \".join([chr(a) for a in range(65, 65 + num_employees)]))\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        st = \"\"\n",
    "        for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "            for s in range(num_shifts):\n",
    "                is_working = solver.Value(works[(e, d, s)])\n",
    "                if is_working:\n",
    "                    a = solver.Value(assignment[(e, d, s)])\n",
    "                    st += f\"{activities[a]:5} \"\n",
    "                else:\n",
    "                    st += \"  *   \"\n",
    "        print(st)\n",
    "        if (d + 1) % 5 == 0:\n",
    "            print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    # Days statistics\n",
    "    # if True:\n",
    "    #     for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "    #         for s in range(num_shifts):\n",
    "    #             st = f\"{d + 1:2},{s} → \"\n",
    "    #             total = 0\n",
    "    #             for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "    #                 nb = 0\n",
    "    #                 for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    #                     if solver.Value(works[(e, d, s)]) and solver.Value(assignment[(e, d, s)]) == a:\n",
    "    #                         nb += 1\n",
    "    #                 total += nb\n",
    "    #                 st += f\"{activities[a]}:{nb} \"\n",
    "    #             print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "    #     print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    # # Employees statistics\n",
    "    # if True:\n",
    "    #     for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    #         st = f\"{chr(65 + e)} → \"\n",
    "    #         total = 0\n",
    "    #         for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "    #             nb = 0\n",
    "    #             for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "    #                 for s in range(num_shifts):\n",
    "    #                     if solver.Value(works[(e, d, s)]) and solver.Value(assignment[(e, d, s)]) == a:\n",
    "    #                         nb += 1\n",
    "    #             total += nb\n",
    "    #             st += f\"{activities[a]:5}:{nb:2} \"\n",
    "    #         print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    print(\"❌ Impossible de satisfaire les contraintes (vérifie les congés et les minima).\")"
   ]
  },

      "N  →  Tél  : 8 Rens : 4 Dérog: 3 Récla: 3 Imp  : 2  (nb activities: 20)\n",

   "source": [
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "import pandas as pd\n",
    "from ortools.sat.python import cp_model\n",
    " \n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Paramètres\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "num_employees = 15\n",
    "employees = [chr(65 + i) for i in range(num_employees)]\n",
    "num_weeks = 4\n",
    "num_days = 5 * num_weeks\n",
    "days = range(num_days)\n",
    "activities = [\"Tél\", \"Rens\", \"Dérog\", \"Récla\", \"Imp\"]\n",
    "num_activities = len(activities)\n",
    "ACT_TEL, ACT_RENS, ACT_DEROG, ACT_RECLA, ACT_IMP = range(num_activities)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes minimales par shift\n",
    "min_staff = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 5,  # Au minimul 5 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 3,  # Au minimul 3 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,  # Au minimul 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,  # Au minimul 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,  # Au minimul 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes maximales par shift\n",
    "max_staff = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 7,  # Pas plus de 7 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 5,  # Pas plus de 5 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,  # Pas plus de 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "max_consec_days = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 2,\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Modèle\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "model = cp_model.CpModel()\n",
    "\n",
    "# Variables : assignment[e][d] = activité (entier 0-4)\n",
    "assignments = {}\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        assignments[(e, d)] = model.NewIntVar(0, num_activities - 1, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : nombre minimal et maximal d'employés par activité par jour\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for d in days:\n",
    "    for a in min_staff:\n",
    "        # Compter combien d'employés font l'activité 'a' ce jour\n",
    "        bools = []\n",
    "        for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'count_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "            bools.append(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) >= min_staff[a])\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_staff[a])\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes du nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for a in max_consec_days:\n",
    "        max_consec = max_consec_days[a]  # maximum de jours consécutifs pour une même activité\n",
    "        for d in range(num_days - max_consec):\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for k in range(max_consec + 1):\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'consec_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}_k{k}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_consec)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : chaque employé doit avoir au moins 3 activités différentes par semaine\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        diff_activities = []\n",
    "        for a in range(num_activities):\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'diff_act_e{e}_w{w}_a{a}')\n",
    "            # b = 1 si l'employé e fait l'activité a au moins un jour de la semaine w\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "                b2 = model.NewBoolVar(f'week_act_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b2)\n",
    "            model.AddMaxEquality(b, bools)\n",
    "            diff_activities.append(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(diff_activities) >= 3)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : chaque employé doit avoir au moins 1 jour de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jours de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jour de renseignement par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de dérog par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de récla par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour d'impayé par semaine\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        bools_tel = []\n",
    "        bools_rens = []\n",
    "        bools_derog = []\n",
    "        bools_recla = []\n",
    "        bools_imp = []\n",
    "        for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "            b_tel = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_rens = model.NewBoolVar(f'rens_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_derog = model.NewBoolVar(f'derog_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_recla = model.NewBoolVar(f'recla_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "            bools_tel.append(b_tel)\n",
    "            bools_rens.append(b_rens)\n",
    "            bools_derog.append(b_derog)\n",
    "            bools_recla.append(b_recla)\n",
    "            bools_imp.append(b_imp)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_tel) <= 2)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_tel) >= 1)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_rens) <= 2)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_derog) <= 1)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_recla) <= 1)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_imp) <= 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : Un employé ne doit pas avoir de téléphone plus de 2 vendredis sur 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    bools_fridays = []\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        d = w * 5 + 4  # Vendredi de la semaine w\n",
    "        b = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_friday_e{e}_w{w}')\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "        bools_fridays.append(b)\n",
    "    model.Add(sum(bools_fridays) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Résolution\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "solver = cp_model.CpSolver()\n",
    "solver.parameters.max_time_in_seconds = 30.0\n",
    "solver.parameters.num_search_workers = 8\n",
    "status = solver.Solve(model)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Affichage\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "if status in (cp_model.FEASIBLE, cp_model.OPTIMAL):\n",
    "    print(\"         \" + \"     \".join([chr(a) for a in range(65, 65 + num_employees)]))\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        st = f\"{d + 1:2}  →  \"\n",
    "        for e in range(num_employees):            \n",
    "            st += f\"{activities[solver.Value(assignment[(e, d)])]:5} \"\n",
    "        print(st)\n",
    "        if (d + 1) % 5 == 0:\n",
    "            print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    # Days statistics\n",
    "    if True:\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics days\")\n",
    "        for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "            st = f\"{d + 1:2}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = 0 #sum([1 for e in range(num_employees) if solver.Value(assignment[(e, d)]) == a])\n",
    "                nb = assignment[(1, d)]\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{activities[a]}:{nb} \"\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    # Employees statistics\n",
    "    if True:\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics employees\")\n",
    "        for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "            st = f\"{chr(65 + e)}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = sum([1 for d in range(num_days) if solver.Value(assignment[(e, d)]) == a])\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{activities[a]:5}:{nb:2} \"\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    print(\"Impossible de satisfaire les contraintes (vérifie les congés et les minima).\")"
   ]
  },

   "source": [
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "import pandas as pd\n",
    "from ortools.sat.python import cp_model\n",
    "\n",
    "class PartialSolutionPrinter(cp_model.CpSolverSolutionCallback):\n",
    "    \"\"\"Print intermediate solutions.\"\"\"\n",
    "\n",
    "    def __init__(self, employees, days, activities, assignments, limit):\n",
    "        cp_model.CpSolverSolutionCallback.__init__(self)\n",
    "        self._employees = employees\n",
    "        self._days = days\n",
    "        self._activities = activities\n",
    "        self._assignments = assignments\n",
    "        self._solution_count = 0\n",
    "        self._solution_limit = limit\n",
    "\n",
    "    def on_solution_callback(self):\n",
    "        self._solution_count += 1\n",
    "        print(f\"Solution {self._solution_count} \" + '-' * 80)\n",
    "        print(\"       \" + \"     \".join(self._employees))\n",
    "\n",
    "        for d in self._days:\n",
    "            st = f\"{d + 1:2} → \"\n",
    "            for e in range(len(self._employees)):\n",
    "                for a in range(len(self._activities)):\n",
    "                    if self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a:\n",
    "                        st += f\"{self._activities[a]:5} \"\n",
    "            print(st)\n",
    "            if (d + 1) % 5 == 0:\n",
    "                print()\n",
    "        self.print_days_statistics()\n",
    "        self.print_employees_statistics()\n",
    "\n",
    "        if self._solution_count >= self._solution_limit:\n",
    "            print(f\"\\nStop search after {self._solution_limit} solutions\")\n",
    "            self.stop_search()\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "    def print_days_statistics(self):\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics days\")\n",
    "        for d in self._days:\n",
    "            st = f\"{d + 1:2}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = sum([1 for e in range(num_employees) if self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a])\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{self._activities[a]} : {nb} \"\n",
    "                toto = 0\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    def print_employees_statistics(self):\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics employees\")\n",
    "        for e in range(len(employees)):\n",
    "            st = f\"{chr(65 + e)}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = sum([1 for d in self._days if self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a])\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{self._activities[a]} : {nb:2} \"\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    def solutionCount(self):\n",
    "        return self._solution_count\n",
    "    \n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Paramètres\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "num_employees = 15\n",
    "employees = [chr(65 + i) for i in range(num_employees)]\n",
    "num_weeks = 4\n",
    "num_days = 5 * num_weeks\n",
    "days = range(num_days)\n",
    "activities = [\"Tél\", \"Rens\", \"Dérog\", \"Récla\", \"Imp\"]\n",
    "num_activities = len(activities)\n",
    "ACT_TEL, ACT_RENS, ACT_DEROG, ACT_RECLA, ACT_IMP = range(num_activities)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes minimales par shift\n",
    "min_staff = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 5,  # Au minimum 5 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 3,  # Au minimum 3 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes maximales par shift\n",
    "max_staff = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 7,  # Pas plus de 7 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 5,  # Pas plus de 5 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,  # Pas plus de 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "max_consec_days = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 2,\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Modèle\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "model = cp_model.CpModel()\n",
    "\n",
    "# Variables : assignment[e][d] = activité (entier 0-4)\n",
    "assignments = {}\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        assignments[(e, d)] = model.NewIntVar(0, num_activities - 1, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : nombre minimal et maximal d'employés par activité par jour\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for d in days:\n",
    "    for a in min_staff:\n",
    "        # Compter combien d'employés font l'activité 'a' ce jour\n",
    "        bools = []\n",
    "        for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'count_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "            bools.append(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) >= min_staff[a])\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_staff[a])\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes du nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for a in max_consec_days:\n",
    "        max_consec = max_consec_days[a]  # maximum de jours consécutifs pour une même activité\n",
    "        for d in range(num_days - max_consec):\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for k in range(max_consec + 1):\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'consec_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}_k{k}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_consec)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : chaque employé doit avoir au moins 3 activités différentes par semaine\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        diff_activities = []\n",
    "        for a in range(num_activities):\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'diff_act_e{e}_w{w}_a{a}')\n",
    "            # b = 1 si l'employé e fait l'activité a au moins un jour de la semaine w\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "                b2 = model.NewBoolVar(f'week_act_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b2)\n",
    "            model.AddMaxEquality(b, bools)\n",
    "            diff_activities.append(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(diff_activities) >= 3)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : chaque employé doit avoir au moins 1 jour de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jours de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jour de renseignement par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de dérog par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de récla par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour d'impayé par semaine\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        bools_tel = []\n",
    "        bools_rens = []\n",
    "        bools_derog = []\n",
    "        bools_recla = []\n",
    "        bools_imp = []\n",
    "        for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "            b_tel = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_rens = model.NewBoolVar(f'rens_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_derog = model.NewBoolVar(f'derog_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_recla = model.NewBoolVar(f'recla_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "            bools_tel.append(b_tel)\n",
    "            bools_rens.append(b_rens)\n",
    "            bools_derog.append(b_derog)\n",
    "            bools_recla.append(b_recla)\n",
    "            bools_imp.append(b_imp)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_tel) <= 2)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_tel) >= 1)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_rens) <= 2)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_derog) <= 1)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_recla) <= 1)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_imp) <= 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : Un employé ne doit pas avoir de téléphone plus de 2 vendredis sur 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    bools_fridays = []\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        d = w * 5 + 4  # Vendredi de la semaine w\n",
    "        b = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_friday_e{e}_w{w}')\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "        bools_fridays.append(b)\n",
    "    model.Add(sum(bools_fridays) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Résolution\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "solver = cp_model.CpSolver()\n",
    "solver.parameters.linearization_level = 0\n",
    "# solver.parameters.max_time_in_seconds = 30.0\n",
    "# solver.parameters.num_search_workers = 8\n",
    "solver.parameters.enumerate_all_solutions = True\n",
    "solution_limit = 5\n",
    "solution_printer = PartialSolutionPrinter(employees, days, activities, assignments, solution_limit)\n",
    "status = solver.Solve(model, solution_printer)"
   ]
  },

   ],
   "source": [
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "import pandas as pd\n",
    "from ortools.sat.python import cp_model\n",
    "\n",
    "class PartialSolutionPrinter(cp_model.CpSolverSolutionCallback):\n",
    "    \"\"\"Print intermediate solutions.\"\"\"\n",
    "\n",
    "    def __init__(self, employees, days, activities, works, assignments, limit):\n",
    "        cp_model.CpSolverSolutionCallback.__init__(self)\n",
    "        self._employees = employees\n",
    "        self._days = days\n",
    "        self._activities = activities\n",
    "        self._assignments = assignments\n",
    "        self._works = works\n",
    "        self._solution_count = 0\n",
    "        self._solution_limit = limit\n",
    "\n",
    "    def on_solution_callback(self):\n",
    "        self._solution_count += 1\n",
    "        print(f\"Solution {self._solution_count} \" + '-' * 80)\n",
    "        print(\"       \" + \"     \".join(self._employees))\n",
    "\n",
    "        for d in self._days:\n",
    "            st = f\"{d + 1:2} → \"\n",
    "            for e in range(len(self._employees)):\n",
    "\n",
    "                if False:\n",
    "                    # First version\n",
    "                    for a in range(len(self._activities)):\n",
    "                        if self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a:\n",
    "                            st += f\"{self._activities[a]:5} \"\n",
    "                else:\n",
    "                    # Second version\n",
    "                    if self.value(self._works[(e, d)]):\n",
    "                        for a in range(len(self._activities)):\n",
    "                            if self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a:\n",
    "                                st += f\"{self._activities[a]:5} \"\n",
    "                    else:\n",
    "                        st += \"  *   \"\n",
    "            print(st)\n",
    "            if (d + 1) % 5 == 0:\n",
    "                print()\n",
    "        self.print_days_statistics()\n",
    "        self.print_employees_statistics()\n",
    "\n",
    "        if self._solution_count >= self._solution_limit:\n",
    "            print(f\"\\nStop search after {self._solution_limit} solutions\")\n",
    "            self.stop_search()\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "    def print_days_statistics(self):\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics days\")\n",
    "        for d in self._days:\n",
    "            st = f\"{d + 1:2}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = sum([1 for e in range(num_employees) if (self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a and self.value(self._works[(e, d)]))])\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{self._activities[a]} : {nb} \"\n",
    "                toto = 0\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    def print_employees_statistics(self):\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics employees\")\n",
    "        for e in range(len(employees)):\n",
    "            st = f\"{chr(65 + e)}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = sum([1 for d in self._days if (self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a and self.value(self._works[(e, d)]))])\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{self._activities[a]} : {nb:2} \"\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    def solutionCount(self):\n",
    "        return self._solution_count\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Paramètres\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "num_employees = 15\n",
    "employees = [chr(65 + i) for i in range(num_employees)]\n",
    "num_weeks = 4\n",
    "num_days = 5 * num_weeks\n",
    "days = range(num_days)\n",
    "activities = [\"Tél\", \"Rens\", \"Dérog\", \"Récla\", \"Imp\"]\n",
    "num_activities = len(activities)\n",
    "ACT_TEL, ACT_RENS, ACT_DEROG, ACT_RECLA, ACT_IMP = range(num_activities)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes minimales par shift\n",
    "min_staff = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 5,  # Au minimum 5 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 3,  # Au minimum 3 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,     # Au minimum 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes maximales par shift\n",
    "max_staff = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 7,  # Pas plus de 7 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 5,  # Pas plus de 5 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,     # Pas plus de 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "max_consec_days = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 2,\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Congés :\n",
    "\n",
    "size = 20\n",
    "conges = set(zip(np.random.choice(np.arange(num_employees - 2), size = size).tolist(), \n",
    "                 np.random.choice(np.arange(num_days), size = size).tolist()))\n",
    "conges.update({(14, i) for i in range(num_days)})  # Employé absent tous les jours\n",
    "# print([f\"{chr(65 + k)} : {v+1}\" for (k, v) in conges if k != 14])\n",
    "\n",
    "num_days_worked = {i : num_days for i in range(num_employees)}\n",
    "print(num_days_worked)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Modèle\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "model = cp_model.CpModel()\n",
    "\n",
    "# ---------------\n",
    "# Variables\n",
    "assignment = {}      # activité si présent\n",
    "works = {}           # booléen : travaille ce shift ?\n",
    "\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        assignment[(e, d)] = model.NewIntVar(0, num_activities - 1, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        works[(e, d)] = model.NewBoolVar(f\"works_e{e}_f{d}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# ---------------\n",
    "# Congés\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        model.Add(works[(e, d)] == int((e, d) not in conges))\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : nombre minimal et maximal d'employés par activité par jour\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for d in days:\n",
    "    for a in min_staff:\n",
    "        # Compter combien d'employés font l'activité 'a' ce jour\n",
    "        bools = []\n",
    "        for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "            if not (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'count_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) >= min_staff[a])\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_staff[a])\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes du nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for a in max_consec_days:\n",
    "        max_consec = max_consec_days[a]  # maximum de jours consécutifs pour une même activité\n",
    "        for d in range(num_days - max_consec):\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for k in range(max_consec + 1):\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'consec_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}_k{k}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_consec)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : chaque employé doit avoir au moins 3 activités différentes par semaine\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        diff_activities = []\n",
    "        num_days_work = 0\n",
    "        for a in range(num_activities):\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'diff_act_e{e}_w{w}_a{a}')\n",
    "            # b = 1 si l'employé e fait l'activité a au moins un jour de la semaine w\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "                # if not (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                #     num_days_work += 1\n",
    "                b2 = model.NewBoolVar(f'week_act_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b2)\n",
    "            model.AddMaxEquality(b, bools)\n",
    "            diff_activities.append(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(diff_activities) >= 3)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : chaque employé doit avoir au moins 1 jour de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jours de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jour de renseignement par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de dérog par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de récla par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour d'impayé par semaine\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        bools_tel = []\n",
    "        bools_rens = []\n",
    "        bools_derog = []\n",
    "        bools_recla = []\n",
    "        bools_imp = []\n",
    "        for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "            b_tel = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_rens = model.NewBoolVar(f'rens_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_derog = model.NewBoolVar(f'derog_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_recla = model.NewBoolVar(f'recla_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "            bools_tel.append(b_tel)\n",
    "            bools_rens.append(b_rens)\n",
    "            bools_derog.append(b_derog)\n",
    "            bools_recla.append(b_recla)\n",
    "            bools_imp.append(b_imp)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_tel) <= 2)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_tel) >= 1)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_rens) <= 2)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_derog) <= 1)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_recla) <= 1)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_imp) <= 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : Pas plus de 2 impayés sur une période de 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    bools_imp_whole_period = []\n",
    "    for d in days:\n",
    "        b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "        bools_imp_whole_period.append(b_imp)\n",
    "    model.Add(sum(bools_imp_whole_period) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : Un employé ne doit pas avoir plus de 2 vendredis en Téléphone sur 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    bools_fridays = []\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        d = w * 5 + 4  # Vendredi de la semaine w\n",
    "        b = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_friday_e{e}_w{w}')\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "        bools_fridays.append(b)\n",
    "    model.Add(sum(bools_fridays) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Résolution\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "solver = cp_model.CpSolver()\n",
    "solver.parameters.linearization_level = 0\n",
    "# solver.parameters.max_time_in_seconds = 30.0\n",
    "# solver.parameters.num_search_workers = 8\n",
    "solver.parameters.enumerate_all_solutions = True\n",
    "solution_limit = 3\n",
    "solution_printer = PartialSolutionPrinter(employees, days, activities, works, assignments, solution_limit)\n",
    "status = solver.Solve(model, solution_printer)\n",
    "print(status)"
   ]
  },

   "source": [
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "import pandas as pd\n",
    "from ortools.sat.python import cp_model\n",
    "\n",
    "class PartialSolutionPrinter(cp_model.CpSolverSolutionCallback):\n",
    "    \"\"\"Print intermediate solutions.\"\"\"\n",
    "\n",
    "    def __init__(self, employees, days, activities, works, assignments, limit):\n",
    "        cp_model.CpSolverSolutionCallback.__init__(self)\n",
    "        self._employees = employees\n",
    "        self._days = days\n",
    "        self._activities = activities\n",
    "        self._assignments = assignments\n",
    "        self._works = works\n",
    "        self._solution_count = 0\n",
    "        self._solution_limit = limit\n",
    "\n",
    "    def on_solution_callback(self):\n",
    "        self._solution_count += 1\n",
    "        print(f\"Solution {self._solution_count}  \" + '-' * 88)\n",
    "        print(\"       \" + \"     \".join(self._employees))\n",
    "\n",
    "        for d in self._days:\n",
    "            st = f\"{d + 1:2} → \"\n",
    "            for e in range(len(self._employees)):\n",
    "                if self.value(self._works[(e, d)]):\n",
    "                    for a in range(len(self._activities)):\n",
    "                        if self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a:\n",
    "                            st += f\"{self._activities[a]:5} \"\n",
    "                else:\n",
    "                    st += \"  *   \"\n",
    "            print(st)\n",
    "            if (d + 1) % 5 == 0:\n",
    "                print()\n",
    "        self.print_days_statistics()\n",
    "        self.print_employees_statistics()\n",
    "\n",
    "        if self._solution_count >= self._solution_limit:\n",
    "            print(f\"\\nStop search after {self._solution_limit} solutions\")\n",
    "            self.stop_search()\n",
    "\n",
    "    def print_days_statistics(self):\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics days\")\n",
    "        for d in self._days:\n",
    "            st = f\"{d + 1:2}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = sum([1 for e in range(num_employees) if (self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a and self.value(self._works[(e, d)]))])\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{self._activities[a]} : {nb} \"\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    def print_employees_statistics(self):\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics employees\")\n",
    "        for e in range(len(employees)):\n",
    "            st = f\"{chr(65 + e)}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = sum([1 for d in self._days if (self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a and self.value(self._works[(e, d)]))])\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{self._activities[a]} : {nb:2} \"\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    def solutionCount(self):\n",
    "        return self._solution_count\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Paramètres\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "num_employees = 15\n",
    "employees = [chr(65 + i) for i in range(num_employees)]\n",
    "num_weeks = 4\n",
    "num_days = 5 * num_weeks\n",
    "days = range(num_days)\n",
    "activities = [\"Tél\", \"Rens\", \"Dérog\", \"Récla\", \"Imp\"]\n",
    "num_activities = len(activities)\n",
    "ACT_TEL, ACT_RENS, ACT_DEROG, ACT_RECLA, ACT_IMP = range(num_activities)\n",
    "ACT_OFF = -1\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes minimales par shift\n",
    "min_staff = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 5,  # Au minimum 5 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 3,  # Au minimum 3 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,     # Au minimum 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes maximales par shift\n",
    "max_staff = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 7,  # Pas plus de 7 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 5,  # Pas plus de 5 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,     # Pas plus de 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "max_consec_days = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 2,\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Congés :\n",
    "\n",
    "size = 20\n",
    "conges = set(zip(np.random.choice(np.arange(num_employees - 2), size = size).tolist(), \n",
    "                 np.random.choice(np.arange(num_days), size = size).tolist()))\n",
    "conges.update({(14, i) for i in range(num_days)})  # Employé absent tous les jours\n",
    "conges.update({(13, i) for i in range(5, 10)}) # Employé absent toute une semaine\n",
    "# print(conges)\n",
    "# print([f\"{chr(65 + k)} : {v+1}\" for (k, v) in conges if k != 14])\n",
    "\n",
    "# num_days_worked = {i : num_days for i in range(num_employees)}\n",
    "# print(num_days_worked)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Modèle\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "model = cp_model.CpModel()\n",
    "\n",
    "# ---------------\n",
    "# Variables\n",
    "assignment = {}      # activité si présent\n",
    "works = {}           # booléen : travaille ce shift ?\n",
    "\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        if (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "            assignment[(e, d)] = model.NewIntVar(ACT_OFF, ACT_OFF, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            assignment[(e, d)] = model.NewIntVar(0, num_activities - 1, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        works[(e, d)] = model.NewBoolVar(f\"works_e{e}_f{d}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# ---------------\n",
    "# Congés\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        model.Add(works[(e, d)] == int((e, d) not in conges))\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : nombre minimal et maximal d'employés par activité par jour\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for d in days:\n",
    "    for a in min_staff:\n",
    "        # Compter combien d'employés font l'activité 'a' ce jour\n",
    "        bools = []\n",
    "        for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "            # if not (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'count_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) >= min_staff[a])\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_staff[a])\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes du nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for a in max_consec_days:\n",
    "        max_consec = max_consec_days[a]  # maximum de jours consécutifs pour une même activité\n",
    "        for d in range(num_days - max_consec):\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for k in range(max_consec + 1):\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'consec_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}_k{k}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_consec)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : Au moins 3 activités différentes par semaine par employé (s'il travaille au moins 3 jours)\n",
    "#                       2  ...                                          (s'il travaille au moins 2 jours) TODO\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        diff_activities = []\n",
    "        num_days_worked_this_week = 0\n",
    "        for a in range(num_activities):\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'diff_act_e{e}_w{w}_a{a}')\n",
    "            # b = 1 si l'employé e fait l'activité a au moins un jour de la semaine w\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "                if not (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                    num_days_worked_this_week += 1\n",
    "                b2 = model.NewBoolVar(f'week_act_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b2)\n",
    "            model.AddMaxEquality(b, bools)\n",
    "            diff_activities.append(b)\n",
    "        min_diff_activities = 3 if num_days_worked_this_week >= 3 else num_days_worked_this_week\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(diff_activities) >= min_diff_activities)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : chaque employé doit avoir au moins 1 jour de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jours de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jour de renseignement par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de dérog par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de récla par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour d'impayé par semaine\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        bools_tel = []\n",
    "        bools_rens = []\n",
    "        bools_derog = []\n",
    "        bools_recla = []\n",
    "        bools_imp = []\n",
    "        work = True\n",
    "        for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "            work = True\n",
    "            if (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                work = False\n",
    "                continue\n",
    "            b_tel = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_rens = model.NewBoolVar(f'rens_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_derog = model.NewBoolVar(f'derog_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_recla = model.NewBoolVar(f'recla_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "            bools_tel.append(b_tel)\n",
    "            bools_rens.append(b_rens)\n",
    "            bools_derog.append(b_derog)\n",
    "            bools_recla.append(b_recla)\n",
    "            bools_imp.append(b_imp)\n",
    "        if work:\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) <= 2)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) >= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_rens) <= 2)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_derog) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_recla) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_imp) <= 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : Pas plus de 2 impayés sur une période de 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    bools_imp_whole_period = []\n",
    "    for d in days:\n",
    "        b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "        bools_imp_whole_period.append(b_imp)\n",
    "    model.Add(sum(bools_imp_whole_period) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : Un employé ne doit pas avoir plus de 2 vendredis en Téléphone sur 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    bools_fridays = []\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        d = w * 5 + 4  # Vendredi de la semaine w\n",
    "        b = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_friday_e{e}_w{w}')\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "        bools_fridays.append(b)\n",
    "    model.Add(sum(bools_fridays) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Résolution\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "solver = cp_model.CpSolver()\n",
    "solver.parameters.linearization_level = 0\n",
    "# solver.parameters.max_time_in_seconds = 30.0\n",
    "# solver.parameters.num_search_workers = 8\n",
    "solver.parameters.enumerate_all_solutions = True\n",
    "solution_limit = 1\n",
    "solution_printer = PartialSolutionPrinter(employees, days, activities, works, assignments, solution_limit)\n",
    "status = solver.Solve(model, solution_printer)\n",
    "print(status)"
   ]
