   "source": [
    "from datetime import date, timedelta, datetime\n",
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "import pandas as pd\n",
    "from ortools.sat.python import cp_model\n",
    "from openpyxl import Workbook\n",
    "from openpyxl.styles import Font, PatternFill, Alignment, Border, Side\n",
    "\n",
    "dict_colors = {\n",
    "    -1: \"AAAAAA\",  # Off\n",
    "    0:  \"FFFF00\",  # Tel\n",
    "    1:  \"FFC901\",  # Rens\n",
    "    2:  \"018CFF\",  # Dérog\n",
    "    3:  \"309C33\",  # Récla\n",
    "    4:  \"FD1913\",  # Imp\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "dict_days = { 0: \"Lundi\", 1: \"Mardi\", 2: \"Mercredi\", 3: \"Jeudi\", 4: \"Vendredi\" }\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "class PartialSolutionPrinter(cp_model.CpSolverSolutionCallback):\n",
    "    \"\"\"Print intermediate solutions.\"\"\"\n",
    "\n",
    "    def __init__(self, employees, days, num_weeks, activities, works, assignments, first_date, now, limit):\n",
    "        cp_model.CpSolverSolutionCallback.__init__(self)\n",
    "        self._employees = employees\n",
    "        self._days = days\n",
    "        self._num_weeks = num_weeks\n",
    "        self._activities = activities\n",
    "        self._assignments = assignments\n",
    "        self._works = works\n",
    "        self._solution_count = 0\n",
    "        self._first_date = first_date\n",
    "        self._now = now\n",
    "        self._solution_limit = limit\n",
    "        self._wb = Workbook()\n",
    "        self._sheet = self._wb.active\n",
    "        self._sheet.title = \"Planning\"\n",
    "\n",
    "    def on_solution_callback(self):\n",
    "        self._solution_count += 1\n",
    "        print(f\"Solution {self._solution_count}  \" + '-' * 88)\n",
    "        print(\"       \" + \"     \".join(self._employees))\n",
    "\n",
    "        cur_row = 2 * (self._solution_count - 1) * (len(self._days) + self._num_weeks) + 1\n",
    "\n",
    "        # Header\n",
    "        self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row, column = 1, value = \"Date\")\n",
    "        self._sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "        self._sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "        for column_idx, employee in enumerate(self._employees, start = 1):\n",
    "            self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row, column = column_idx + 3, value = employee)\n",
    "            self._sheet[f\"{chr(65 + column_idx + 2)}{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "            self._sheet[f\"{chr(65 + column_idx + 2)}{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "\n",
    "        cur_date = self._first_date\n",
    "        cur_row += 1\n",
    "        for w in range(self._num_weeks):\n",
    "            for i in range(5):\n",
    "                d = 5 * w + i\n",
    "                st = f\"{d + 1:2} → \"\n",
    "                st_date = cur_date.strftime(\"%d/%m/%y\")\n",
    "                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row,  column = 1, value = st_date)\n",
    "                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row,  column = 2, value = dict_days[i])\n",
    "                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row,  column = 3, value = \"M\")\n",
    "                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row + 1,  column = 3, value = \"AM\")\n",
    "                self._sheet.merge_cells(start_row = cur_row, start_column = 1, end_row = cur_row + 1, end_column = 1)\n",
    "                self._sheet.merge_cells(start_row = cur_row, start_column = 2, end_row = cur_row + 1, end_column = 2)\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"B{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"C{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"C{cur_row + 1}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"B{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"C{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"C{cur_row + 1}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                self._sheet.column_dimensions['A'].width = len(str(\"--------------\"))\n",
    "                self._sheet.column_dimensions['B'].width = len(str(\"--------------\"))\n",
    "                self._sheet.row_dimensions[cur_row].height = 14\n",
    "                self._sheet.row_dimensions[cur_row + 1].height = 14\n",
    "                cur_date += timedelta(days = 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "                for e in range(len(self._employees)):\n",
    "                    if self.value(self._works[(e, d)]):\n",
    "                        for a in range(len(self._activities)):\n",
    "                            if self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a:\n",
    "                                st += f\"{self._activities[a]:5} \"\n",
    "                                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row,  column = e + 4, value = self._activities[a])\n",
    "                                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row + 1,  column = e + 4, value = self._activities[a])\n",
    "                                self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[a], end_color=dict_colors[a], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "                                self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row + 1}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[a], end_color=dict_colors[a], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "                                self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                                self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row + 1}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                    else:\n",
    "                        st += \"  *   \"\n",
    "                        self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[-1], end_color=dict_colors[-1], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "                        self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row + 1}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[-1], end_color=dict_colors[-1], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "                print(st)\n",
    "                cur_row += 2\n",
    "            PartialSolutionPrinter.set_border(self._sheet, f\"A{cur_row - 10}:{chr(67 + len(self._employees))}{cur_row - 1}\")\n",
    "            print()\n",
    "            cur_row += 1\n",
    "            cur_date += timedelta(days = 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "        self.print_days_statistics()\n",
    "        self.print_employees_statistics()\n",
    "\n",
    "        if self._solution_count >= self._solution_limit:\n",
    "            print(f\"\\nStop search after {self._solution_limit} solutions\")\n",
    "            self.stop_search()\n",
    "            # Save Excel file\n",
    "            # print(f\"{now.year} {now.month} {now.day} {now.hour} {now.minute}\")\n",
    "            self._wb.save(f\"Planning_{now.year}_{now.month}_{now.day}_{now.hour}_{now.minute}.xlsx\")\n",
    "\n",
    "    @staticmethod\n",
    "    def set_border(ws, cell_range):\n",
    "        thin = Side(border_style=\"thin\", color=\"000000\")\n",
    "        for row in ws[cell_range]:\n",
    "            for cell in row:\n",
    "                cell.border = Border(top=thin, left=thin, right=thin, bottom=thin)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "    def print_days_statistics(self):\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics days\")\n",
    "        for d in self._days:\n",
    "            st = f\"{d + 1:2}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = sum([1 for e in range(num_employees) if (self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a and self.value(self._works[(e, d)]))])\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{self._activities[a]} : {nb} \"\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    def print_employees_statistics(self):\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics employees\")\n",
    "        for e in range(len(employees)):\n",
    "            st = f\"{chr(65 + e)}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = sum([1 for d in self._days if (self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a and self.value(self._works[(e, d)]))])\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{self._activities[a]} : {nb:2} \"\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    def solutionCount(self):\n",
    "        return self._solution_count\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Paramètres\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "num_employees = 15\n",
    "num_weeks = 4\n",
    "num_days = 5 * num_weeks\n",
    "employees = [chr(65 + i) for i in range(num_employees)]\n",
    "days = range(num_days)\n",
    "first_date = date(2025, 10, 20)\n",
    "st = first_date.strftime(\"%d/%m/%y\")\n",
    "print(\"DATE: \", first_date, st)\n",
    "\n",
    "activities = [\"Tél\", \"Rens\", \"Dérog\", \"Récla\", \"Imp\"]\n",
    "num_activities = len(activities)\n",
    "ACT_TEL, ACT_RENS, ACT_DEROG, ACT_RECLA, ACT_IMP = range(num_activities)\n",
    "ACT_OFF = -1\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes minimales par shift\n",
    "min_staff = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 5,  # Au minimum 5 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 3,  # Au minimum 3 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,     # Au minimum 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes maximales par shift\n",
    "max_staff = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 7,  # Pas plus de 7 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 5,  # Pas plus de 5 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,     # Pas plus de 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "max_consec_days = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 2,\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Congés :\n",
    "\n",
    "size = 20\n",
    "conges = set(zip(np.random.choice(np.arange(num_employees - 2), size = size).tolist(),\n",
    "                 np.random.choice(np.arange(num_days), size = size).tolist()))\n",
    "conges.update({(14, i) for i in range(num_days)})  # Employé absent tous les jours\n",
    "conges.update({(1, i) for i in range(5, 10)}) # Employé absent toute une semaine\n",
    "\n",
    "# num_days_worked = {i : num_days for i in range(num_employees)}\n",
    "# print(num_days_worked)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Modèle\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "model = cp_model.CpModel()\n",
    "\n",
    "# ---------------\n",
    "# Variables\n",
    "assignments = {}      # activité si présent\n",
    "works = {}           # booléen : travaille ce shift ?\n",
    "\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        if (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "            assignments[(e, d)] = model.NewIntVar(ACT_OFF, ACT_OFF, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            assignments[(e, d)] = model.NewIntVar(0, num_activities - 1, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        works[(e, d)] = model.NewBoolVar(f\"works_e{e}_f{d}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# ---------------\n",
    "# Congés\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        model.Add(works[(e, d)] == int((e, d) not in conges))\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : nombre minimal et maximal d'employés par activité par jour\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for d in days:\n",
    "    for a in min_staff:\n",
    "        # Compter combien d'employés font l'activité 'a' ce jour\n",
    "        bools = []\n",
    "        for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "            # if not (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'count_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) >= min_staff[a])\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_staff[a])\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes du nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for a in max_consec_days:\n",
    "        max_consec = max_consec_days[a]  # maximum de jours consécutifs pour une même activité\n",
    "        for d in range(num_days - max_consec):\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for k in range(max_consec + 1):\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'consec_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}_k{k}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_consec)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : Au moins 3 activités différentes par semaine par employé (s'il travaille au moins 3 jours)\n",
    "#                       2  ...                                          (s'il travaille au moins 2 jours) TODO\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        diff_activities = []\n",
    "        num_days_worked_this_week = 0\n",
    "        for a in range(num_activities):\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'diff_act_e{e}_w{w}_a{a}')\n",
    "            # b = 1 si l'employé e fait l'activité a au moins un jour de la semaine w\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "                if not (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                    num_days_worked_this_week += 1\n",
    "                b2 = model.NewBoolVar(f'week_act_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b2)\n",
    "            model.AddMaxEquality(b, bools)\n",
    "            diff_activities.append(b)\n",
    "        min_diff_activities = 3 if num_days_worked_this_week >= 3 else num_days_worked_this_week\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(diff_activities) >= min_diff_activities)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : chaque employé doit avoir au moins 1 jour de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jours de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jour de renseignement par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de dérog par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de récla par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour d'impayé par semaine\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        bools_tel = []\n",
    "        bools_rens = []\n",
    "        bools_derog = []\n",
    "        bools_recla = []\n",
    "        bools_imp = []\n",
    "        work = True\n",
    "        for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "            work = True\n",
    "            # Not accurage\n",
    "            # Max and min number of activities should depend on the number of working days per employee\n",
    "            if (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                work = False\n",
    "                continue\n",
    "            b_tel = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_rens = model.NewBoolVar(f'rens_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_derog = model.NewBoolVar(f'derog_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_recla = model.NewBoolVar(f'recla_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "            bools_tel.append(b_tel)\n",
    "            bools_rens.append(b_rens)\n",
    "            bools_derog.append(b_derog)\n",
    "            bools_recla.append(b_recla)\n",
    "            bools_imp.append(b_imp)\n",
    "        if work:\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) <= 2)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) >= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_rens) <= 2)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_derog) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_recla) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_imp) <= 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : Pas plus de 2 impayés sur une période de 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    bools_imp_whole_period = []\n",
    "    for d in days:\n",
    "        b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "        bools_imp_whole_period.append(b_imp)\n",
    "    model.Add(sum(bools_imp_whole_period) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : Un employé ne doit pas avoir plus de 2 vendredis en Téléphone sur 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    bools_fridays = []\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        d = w * 5 + 4  # Vendredi de la semaine w\n",
    "        b = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_friday_e{e}_w{w}')\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "        bools_fridays.append(b)\n",
    "    model.Add(sum(bools_fridays) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "now = datetime.now()\n",
    "print(f\"{now.year} {now.month} {now.day} {now.hour} {now.minute}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Résolution\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "solver = cp_model.CpSolver()\n",
    "solver.parameters.linearization_level = 0\n",
    "# solver.parameters.max_time_in_seconds = 30.0\n",
    "# solver.parameters.num_search_workers = 8\n",
    "solver.parameters.enumerate_all_solutions = True\n",
    "solution_limit = 5\n",
    "solution_printer = PartialSolutionPrinter(employees, days, num_weeks, activities, works, assignments, first_date, now, solution_limit)\n",
    "status = solver.Solve(model, solution_printer)\n",
    "print(status)"
   ]
  },

   "source": [
    "import os\n",
    "import time\n",
    "from datetime import date, timedelta, datetime\n",
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "import pandas as pd\n",
    "from ortools.sat.python import cp_model\n",
    "from openpyxl import Workbook\n",
    "from openpyxl.styles import Font, PatternFill, Alignment, Border, Side\n",
    "\n",
    "dict_colors = {\n",
    "    -1: \"AAAAAA\",  # Off\n",
    "    0:  \"FFFF00\",  # Tel\n",
    "    1:  \"FFC901\",  # Rens\n",
    "    2:  \"018CFF\",  # Dérog\n",
    "    3:  \"309C33\",  # Récla\n",
    "    4:  \"FD1913\",  # Imp\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "dict_days = { 0: \"Lundi\", 1: \"Mardi\", 2: \"Mercredi\", 3: \"Jeudi\", 4: \"Vendredi\" }\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "class PartialSolutionPrinter(cp_model.CpSolverSolutionCallback):\n",
    "    \"\"\"Print intermediate solutions.\"\"\"\n",
    "\n",
    "    def __init__(self, employees, days, num_weeks, activities, assignments, conges, first_date, now, limit):\n",
    "        cp_model.CpSolverSolutionCallback.__init__(self)\n",
    "        self._employees = employees\n",
    "        self._days = days\n",
    "        self._num_weeks = num_weeks\n",
    "        self._activities = activities\n",
    "        self._assignments = assignments\n",
    "        self._conges = conges\n",
    "        self._solution_count = 0\n",
    "        self._first_date = first_date\n",
    "        self._now = now\n",
    "        self._solution_limit = limit\n",
    "        self._wb = Workbook()\n",
    "        self._sheet = self._wb.active\n",
    "        self._sheet.title = \"Planning\"\n",
    "        self._arr_solutions = np.empty(shape = (1, len(employees)))\n",
    "        self._test_numpy = False\n",
    "\n",
    "    def on_solution_callback(self):\n",
    "        self._solution_count += 1\n",
    "        print(f\"Solution {self._solution_count}  \" + '-' * 88)\n",
    "        print(\"       \" + \"     \".join(self._employees))\n",
    "\n",
    "        cur_row = 2 * (self._solution_count - 1) * (len(self._days) + self._num_weeks) + 1\n",
    "\n",
    "        if self._test_numpy:\n",
    "            arr = np.empty(shape = (len(days), len(employees)), dtype = int)\n",
    "            for d in days:\n",
    "                row = []\n",
    "                for e in range(len(employees)):\n",
    "                    row.append(self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]))\n",
    "                arr[d] = row\n",
    "            \n",
    "            self._arr_solutions = np.concat([self._arr_solutions, arr])\n",
    "            if self._solution_count == 1:\n",
    "                self._arr_solutions = np.delete(self._arr_solutions, 0, 0)\n",
    "\n",
    "        # Header\n",
    "        self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row, column = 1, value = \"Date\")\n",
    "        self._sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "        self._sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "        for column_idx, employee in enumerate(self._employees, start = 1):\n",
    "            self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row, column = column_idx + 3, value = employee)\n",
    "            self._sheet[f\"{chr(65 + column_idx + 2)}{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "            self._sheet[f\"{chr(65 + column_idx + 2)}{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "\n",
    "        cur_date = self._first_date\n",
    "        cur_row += 1\n",
    "        for w in range(self._num_weeks):\n",
    "            for i in range(5):\n",
    "                d = 5 * w + i\n",
    "                st = f\"{d + 1:2} → \"\n",
    "                st_date = cur_date.strftime(\"%d/%m/%y\")\n",
    "                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row,  column = 1, value = st_date)\n",
    "                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row,  column = 2, value = dict_days[i])\n",
    "                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row,  column = 3, value = \"M\")\n",
    "                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row + 1,  column = 3, value = \"AM\")\n",
    "                self._sheet.merge_cells(start_row = cur_row, start_column = 1, end_row = cur_row + 1, end_column = 1)\n",
    "                self._sheet.merge_cells(start_row = cur_row, start_column = 2, end_row = cur_row + 1, end_column = 2)\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"B{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"C{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"C{cur_row + 1}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"B{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"C{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                self._sheet[f\"C{cur_row + 1}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                self._sheet.column_dimensions['A'].width = len(str(\"--------------\"))\n",
    "                self._sheet.column_dimensions['B'].width = len(str(\"--------------\"))\n",
    "                self._sheet.row_dimensions[cur_row].height = 14\n",
    "                self._sheet.row_dimensions[cur_row + 1].height = 14\n",
    "                cur_date += timedelta(days = 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "                for e in range(len(self._employees)):\n",
    "                    if not (e, d) in self._conges:\n",
    "                        for a in range(len(self._activities)):\n",
    "                            if self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a:\n",
    "                                st += f\"{self._activities[a]:5} \"\n",
    "                                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row,  column = e + 4, value = self._activities[a])\n",
    "                                self._sheet.cell(row = cur_row + 1,  column = e + 4, value = self._activities[a])\n",
    "                                self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[a], end_color=dict_colors[a], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "                                self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row + 1}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[a], end_color=dict_colors[a], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "                                self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                                self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row + 1}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                    else:\n",
    "                        st += \"  *   \"\n",
    "                        self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[-1], end_color=dict_colors[-1], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "                        self._sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row + 1}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[-1], end_color=dict_colors[-1], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "                print(st)\n",
    "                cur_row += 2\n",
    "            PartialSolutionPrinter.set_border(self._sheet, f\"A{cur_row - 10}:{chr(67 + len(self._employees))}{cur_row - 1}\")\n",
    "            print()\n",
    "            cur_row += 1\n",
    "            cur_date += timedelta(days = 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "        self.print_days_statistics()\n",
    "        self.print_employees_statistics()\n",
    "\n",
    "        if self._solution_count >= self._solution_limit:\n",
    "            print(f\"\\nStop search after {self._solution_limit} solutions\")\n",
    "            self.stop_search()\n",
    "            # Display solutions as numpy array (To check differences)\n",
    "            if self._test_numpy:\n",
    "                for i in range(self._solution_count - 1):\n",
    "                    arr1 = self._arr_solutions[i * len(days):(i + 1) * len(days)]\n",
    "                    for j in range(i + 1, self._solution_count):\n",
    "                        arr2 = self._arr_solutions[j * len(days):(j + 1) * len(days)]\n",
    "                    if not np.all(arr1 == arr2):\n",
    "                        print(arr1)\n",
    "                        print(arr2)\n",
    "                    print('-' * 80)\n",
    "                # print(self._arr_solutions)\n",
    "            # Save Excel file\n",
    "            filename = f\"Results\\\\Planning_{now.year}-{now.month}-{now.day}_{now.hour}h{now.minute}.xlsx\"\n",
    "            self._wb.save(filename)\n",
    "            time.sleep(5)\n",
    "            os.system(filename)\n",
    "\n",
    "    @staticmethod\n",
    "    def set_border(ws, cell_range):\n",
    "        thin = Side(border_style=\"thin\", color=\"000000\")\n",
    "        for row in ws[cell_range]:\n",
    "            for cell in row:\n",
    "                cell.border = Border(top=thin, left=thin, right=thin, bottom=thin)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "    def print_days_statistics(self):\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics days\")\n",
    "        for d in self._days:\n",
    "            st = f\"{d + 1:2}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = sum([1 for e in range(num_employees) if (self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a and (e, d) not in self._conges)])\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{self._activities[a]} : {nb} \"\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    def print_employees_statistics(self):\n",
    "        print(\"Statistics employees\")\n",
    "        for e in range(len(employees)):\n",
    "            st = f\"{chr(65 + e)}  →  \"\n",
    "            total = 0\n",
    "            for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                nb = sum([1 for d in self._days if (self.value(self._assignments[(e, d)]) == a and (e, d) not in self._conges)])\n",
    "                total += nb\n",
    "                st += f\"{self._activities[a]} : {nb:2} \"\n",
    "            print(st + f\" (nb activities: {total})\")\n",
    "        print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    def solutionCount(self):\n",
    "        return self._solution_count\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Paramètres\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "num_employees = 15\n",
    "num_weeks = 4\n",
    "num_days = 5 * num_weeks\n",
    "employees = [chr(65 + i) for i in range(num_employees)]\n",
    "days = range(num_days)\n",
    "first_date = date(2025, 10, 20)\n",
    "\n",
    "activities = [\"Tél\", \"Rens\", \"Dérog\", \"Récla\", \"Imp\"]\n",
    "num_activities = len(activities)\n",
    "ACT_TEL, ACT_RENS, ACT_DEROG, ACT_RECLA, ACT_IMP = range(num_activities)\n",
    "ACT_OFF = -1\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes minimales par shift\n",
    "min_staff_per_act = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 5,  # Au minimum 5 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 3,  # Au minimum 3 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,     # Au minimum 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes maximales par shift\n",
    "max_staff_per_act = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 7,  # Pas plus de 7 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 5,  # Pas plus de 5 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,     # Pas plus de 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "max_consec_days = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 2,\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes du nombre d'activités par semaine (en fonction du nombre de jours travaillés)\n",
    "min_diff_activities = {\n",
    "# nb day: min number of different activities\n",
    "    1: 1,\n",
    "    2: 2,\n",
    "    3: 3,\n",
    "    4: 3,\n",
    "    5: 3\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Congés :\n",
    "\n",
    "size = 5\n",
    "conges = set(zip(np.random.choice(np.arange(num_employees - 2), size = size).tolist(),\n",
    "                 np.random.choice(np.arange(num_days), size = size).tolist()))\n",
    "conges.update({(14, i) for i in range(num_days)})  # Employé absent tous les jours\n",
    "conges.update({(1, i) for i in range(5, 10)}) # Employé absent toute une semaine\n",
    "conges.update({(2, 2 + 5 * w) for w in range(num_weeks)}) # Employé absent tous les mercredis\n",
    "conges.update({(10, 2 + 5 * w) for w in range(num_weeks)}) # Employé absent tous les mercredis\n",
    "conges.update({(4, 4 + 5 * w) for w in range(num_weeks)}) # Employé absent tous les vendredis\n",
    "\n",
    "# num_days_worked = {i : num_days for i in range(num_employees)}\n",
    "# print(num_days_worked)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Modèle\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "model = cp_model.CpModel()\n",
    "\n",
    "# ---------------\n",
    "# Variables\n",
    "# ---------------\n",
    "assignments = {}      # activité si présent\n",
    "\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        if (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "            assignments[(e, d)] = model.NewIntVar(ACT_OFF, ACT_OFF, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            assignments[(e, d)] = model.NewIntVar(0, num_activities - 1, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : nombre minimal et maximal d'employés par activité par jour\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for d in days:\n",
    "    for a in min_staff_per_act:\n",
    "        # Compter combien d'employés font l'activité 'a' ce jour\n",
    "        bools = []\n",
    "        for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'count_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "            bools.append(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) >= min_staff_per_act[a])\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_staff_per_act[a])\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes du nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for a in max_consec_days:\n",
    "        # maximum de jours consécutifs pour une même activité\n",
    "        max_consec = max_consec_days[a]\n",
    "        for d in range(num_days - max_consec):\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for k in range(max_consec + 1):\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'consec_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}_k{k}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_consec)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : Au moins 3 activités différentes par semaine par employé (s'il travaille au moins 3 jours)\n",
    "#                       2  ...                                          (s'il travaille au moins 2 jours) TODO\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        diff_activities = []\n",
    "        num_days_worked_this_week = sum([int(not (e, d) in conges) for d in range(5 * w, 5 * (w + 1))])\n",
    "        for a in range(num_activities):\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'diff_act_e{e}_w{w}_a{a}')\n",
    "            # b = 1 si l'employé e fait l'activité a au moins un jour de la semaine w\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "                # if not (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                #     num_days_worked_this_week += 1\n",
    "                b2 = model.NewBoolVar(f'week_act_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b2)\n",
    "            model.AddMaxEquality(b, bools)\n",
    "            diff_activities.append(b)\n",
    "        # min_diff_activities = 3 if num_days_worked_this_week >= 3 else num_days_worked_this_week\n",
    "        if num_days_worked_this_week:\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(diff_activities) >= min_diff_activities[num_days_worked_this_week])\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : chaque employé doit avoir au moins 1 jour de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jours de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jour de renseignement par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de dérog par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de récla par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour d'impayé par semaine\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        bools_tel = []\n",
    "        bools_rens = []\n",
    "        bools_derog = []\n",
    "        bools_recla = []\n",
    "        bools_imp = []\n",
    "        number_working_days = 0\n",
    "        for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "            if (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                continue\n",
    "            number_working_days += 1\n",
    "            b_tel = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_rens = model.NewBoolVar(f'rens_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_derog = model.NewBoolVar(f'derog_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_recla = model.NewBoolVar(f'recla_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "            bools_tel.append(b_tel)\n",
    "            bools_rens.append(b_rens)\n",
    "            bools_derog.append(b_derog)\n",
    "            bools_recla.append(b_recla)\n",
    "            bools_imp.append(b_imp)\n",
    "        # Number of activities per week depends on number of working days\n",
    "        if number_working_days == 0:\n",
    "            # Not working at all\n",
    "            pass\n",
    "        elif number_working_days == 1:\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_rens) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_derog) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_recla) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_imp) <= 1)\n",
    "        elif number_working_days <= 3:\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) <= 2)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) >= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_rens) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_derog) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_recla) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_imp) <= 1)\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            # number_working_days <= 5:\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) <= 2)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) >= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_rens) <= 2)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_derog) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_recla) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_imp) <= 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : Pas plus de 2 impayés sur une période de 4 semaines\n",
    "#              Au moins 1 fois des impayés sur une période de 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    number_working_days = sum([int(not (e, d) in conges) for d in days])\n",
    "    bools_imp_whole_period = []\n",
    "    for d in days:\n",
    "        b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "        bools_imp_whole_period.append(b_imp)\n",
    "    if number_working_days >= 10:\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_imp_whole_period) >= 1)\n",
    "    model.Add(sum(bools_imp_whole_period) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : Pas d'impayés 2 semaines de suite\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# TODO\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : Un employé ne doit pas avoir plus de 2 vendredis en Téléphone sur 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    bools_fridays = []\n",
    "    number_fridays = 0\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        friday = 4 + 5 * w\n",
    "        if not (e, friday) in conges:\n",
    "            number_fridays += 1\n",
    "    if number_fridays >= 3:\n",
    "        for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "            friday = 4 + w * 5\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_friday_e{e}_w{w}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, friday)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, friday)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "            bools_fridays.append(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_fridays) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "now = datetime.now()\n",
    "print(f\"{now.year}-{now.month}-{now.day}_{now.hour}h{now.minute}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Résolution\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "solver = cp_model.CpSolver()\n",
    "solver.parameters.linearization_level = 0\n",
    "# solver.parameters.max_time_in_seconds = 30.0\n",
    "# solver.parameters.num_search_workers = 8\n",
    "solver.parameters.enumerate_all_solutions = True\n",
    "solution_limit = 3\n",
    "solution_printer = PartialSolutionPrinter(employees, days, num_weeks, activities, assignments, \n",
    "                                          conges, first_date, now, solution_limit)\n",
    "\n",
    "status = solver.Solve(model, solution_printer)\n",
    "print(status)"
   ]
  },

    "<div style=\"\n",

    "    <h3 style=\"\n",
    "        color: #2e3a59;\n",
    "        font-family: 'Segoe UI', sans-serif;\n",
    "        margin: 0;\n",
    "        font-weight: 500;\n",
    "    \">\n",
    "    Add Random Seed to generate \"very different\" plannings.<br>\n",
    "    </h3>\n",
    "</div>\n",
    "\n",
    "Without using seeds, the generated plannings all look the same (only one or 2 shifts changed)<br>\n",
    "We should generate, let's say, 5 plannings with 5 different seeds (to be sure to get cery different plannings).<br>\n",
    "Add constraint : No 2 consecutive fridays on \"Tel\""

   "source": [
    "import os\n",
    "import time\n",
    "from datetime import date, timedelta, datetime\n",
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "import pandas as pd\n",
    "from ortools.sat.python import cp_model\n",
    "from openpyxl import Workbook\n",
    "from openpyxl.styles import Font, PatternFill, Alignment, Border, Side\n",
    "\n",
    "dict_colors = {\n",
    "    -1: \"AAAAAA\",  # Off\n",
    "    0:  \"FFFF00\",  # Tel\n",
    "    1:  \"FFC901\",  # Rens\n",
    "    2:  \"018CFF\",  # Dérog\n",
    "    3:  \"309C33\",  # Récla\n",
    "    4:  \"FD1913\",  # Imp\n",
    "    5:  \"5AF4DA\",  # Header Planning n°\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "thin = Side(border_style=\"thin\", color=\"000000\")\n",
    "\n",
    "dict_days = { 0: \"Lundi\", 1: \"Mardi\", 2: \"Mercredi\", 3: \"Jeudi\", 4: \"Vendredi\" }\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Paramètres\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "num_employees = 15\n",
    "num_weeks = 4\n",
    "num_days = 5 * num_weeks\n",
    "employees = [chr(65 + i) for i in range(num_employees)]\n",
    "days = range(num_days)\n",
    "first_date = date(2025, 10, 20)\n",
    "\n",
    "activities = [\"Tél\", \"Rens\", \"Dérog\", \"Récla\", \"Imp\"]\n",
    "num_activities = len(activities)\n",
    "ACT_TEL, ACT_RENS, ACT_DEROG, ACT_RECLA, ACT_IMP = range(num_activities)\n",
    "ACT_OFF = -1\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes minimales par shift\n",
    "min_staff_per_act = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 5,  # Au minimum 5 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 3,  # Au minimum 3 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,  # Au minimum 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,     # Au minimum 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes maximales par shift\n",
    "max_staff_per_act = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 7,  # Pas plus de 7 en Téléphone\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 5,  # Pas plus de 5 en Renseignement\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Dérogation\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 2,  # Pas plus de 1 en Réclamation\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,     # Pas plus de 1 en Impayés\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "max_consec_days = {\n",
    "    ACT_TEL: 2,\n",
    "    ACT_RENS: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_DEROG: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_RECLA: 1,\n",
    "    ACT_IMP: 1,\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# Contraintes du nombre d'activités par semaine (en fonction du nombre de jours travaillés)\n",
    "min_diff_activities = {\n",
    "# nb day: min number of different activities\n",
    "    1: 1,\n",
    "    2: 2,\n",
    "    3: 3,\n",
    "    4: 3,\n",
    "    5: 3\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Congés :\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "size = 5\n",
    "# FIRST VERSION\n",
    "conges = set(zip(np.random.choice(np.arange(num_employees - 2), size = size).tolist(),\n",
    "                 np.random.choice(np.arange(num_days), size = size).tolist()))\n",
    "conges.update({(14, i) for i in range(num_days)})  # Employé absent tous les jours\n",
    "conges.update({(1, i) for i in range(5, 10)}) # Employé absent toute une semaine\n",
    "conges.update({(2, 2 + 5 * w) for w in range(num_weeks)}) # Employé absent tous les mercredis\n",
    "conges.update({(10, 2 + 5 * w) for w in range(num_weeks)}) # Employé absent tous les mercredis\n",
    "conges.update({(4, 4 + 5 * w) for w in range(num_weeks)}) # Employé absent tous les vendredis\n",
    "\n",
    "random_list_1 = np.random.choice(np.arange(num_employees - 2), size = size).tolist()\n",
    "random_list_2 = np.random.choice(np.arange(num_days), size = size).tolist()\n",
    "conges2 = set(zip(random_list_1, random_list_2, 0))\n",
    "conges2.update(set(zip(random_list_1, random_list_2, 0)))\n",
    "\n",
    "conges2.update({(14, i, 0) for i in range(num_days)})  # Employé absent tous les jours\n",
    "conges2.update({(14, i, 1) for i in range(num_days)})\n",
    "conges2.update({(1, i, 0) for i in range(5, 10)}) # Employé absent toute une semaine\n",
    "conges2.update({(1, i, 1) for i in range(5, 10)})\n",
    "conges2.update({(2, 2 + 5 * w, 0) for w in range(num_weeks)}) # Employé absent tous les mercredis\n",
    "conges2.update({(2, 2 + 5 * w, 1) for w in range(num_weeks)})\n",
    "conges2.update({(10, 2 + 5 * w, 0) for w in range(num_weeks)}) # Employé absent tous les mercredis\n",
    "conges2.update({(10, 2 + 5 * w, 1) for w in range(num_weeks)})\n",
    "conges2.update({(4, 4 + 5 * w, 0) for w in range(num_weeks)}) # Employé absent tous les vendredis\n",
    "conges2.update({(4, 4 + 5 * w, 1) for w in range(num_weeks)})\n",
    "\n",
    "conges = {(i, j) for (i, j, k) in conges2}\n",
    "\n",
    "# num_days_worked = {i : num_days for i in range(num_employees)}\n",
    "# print(num_days_worked)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Modèle\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "model = cp_model.CpModel()\n",
    "\n",
    "# ---------------\n",
    "# Variables\n",
    "# ---------------\n",
    "assignments = {}      # activité si présent\n",
    "\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for d in range(num_days):\n",
    "        if (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "            assignments[(e, d)] = model.NewIntVar(ACT_OFF, ACT_OFF, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            assignments[(e, d)] = model.NewIntVar(0, num_activities - 1, f'assign_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : nombre minimal et maximal d'employés par activité par jour\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for d in days:\n",
    "    for a in min_staff_per_act:\n",
    "        # Compter combien d'employés font l'activité 'a' ce jour\n",
    "        bools = []\n",
    "        for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'count_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "            bools.append(b)\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) >= min_staff_per_act[a])\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_staff_per_act[a])\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes du nombre de jours consécutifs maximal\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for a in max_consec_days:\n",
    "        # maximum de jours consécutifs pour une même activité\n",
    "        max_consec = max_consec_days[a]\n",
    "        for d in range(num_days - max_consec):\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for k in range(max_consec + 1):\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'consec_e{e}_d{d}_a{a}_k{k}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d + k)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools) <= max_consec)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : Au moins 3 activités différentes par semaine par employé (s'il travaille au moins 3 jours)\n",
    "#                       2  ...                                          (s'il travaille au moins 2 jours) TODO\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        diff_activities = []\n",
    "        num_days_worked_this_week = sum([int(not (e, d) in conges) for d in range(5 * w, 5 * (w + 1))])\n",
    "        for a in range(num_activities):\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'diff_act_e{e}_w{w}_a{a}')\n",
    "            # b = 1 si l'employé e fait l'activité a au moins un jour de la semaine w\n",
    "            bools = []\n",
    "            for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "                # if not (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                #     num_days_worked_this_week += 1\n",
    "                b2 = model.NewBoolVar(f'week_act_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}_a{a}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != a).OnlyEnforceIf(b2.Not())\n",
    "                bools.append(b2)\n",
    "            model.AddMaxEquality(b, bools)\n",
    "            diff_activities.append(b)\n",
    "        # min_diff_activities = 3 if num_days_worked_this_week >= 3 else num_days_worked_this_week\n",
    "        if num_days_worked_this_week:\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(diff_activities) >= min_diff_activities[num_days_worked_this_week])\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : chaque employé doit avoir au moins 1 jour de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jours de Téléphone par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 2 jour de renseignement par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de dérog par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour de récla par semaine\n",
    "#                                      au maximum 1 jour d'impayé par semaine\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "        bools_tel = []\n",
    "        bools_rens = []\n",
    "        bools_derog = []\n",
    "        bools_recla = []\n",
    "        bools_imp = []\n",
    "        number_working_days = 0\n",
    "        for d in range(w * 5, (w + 1) * 5):\n",
    "            if (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                continue\n",
    "            number_working_days += 1\n",
    "            b_tel = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_rens = model.NewBoolVar(f'rens_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_derog = model.NewBoolVar(f'derog_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_recla = model.NewBoolVar(f'recla_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_w{w}_d{d}')\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b_tel.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RENS).OnlyEnforceIf(b_rens.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_DEROG).OnlyEnforceIf(b_derog.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_RECLA).OnlyEnforceIf(b_recla.Not())\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "            bools_tel.append(b_tel)\n",
    "            bools_rens.append(b_rens)\n",
    "            bools_derog.append(b_derog)\n",
    "            bools_recla.append(b_recla)\n",
    "            bools_imp.append(b_imp)\n",
    "        # Number of activities per week depends on number of working days\n",
    "        if number_working_days == 0:\n",
    "            # Not working at all\n",
    "            pass\n",
    "        elif number_working_days == 1:\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_rens) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_derog) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_recla) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_imp) <= 1)\n",
    "        elif number_working_days <= 3:\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) <= 2)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) >= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_rens) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_derog) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_recla) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_imp) <= 1)\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            # number_working_days <= 5:\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) <= 2)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_tel) >= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_rens) <= 2)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_derog) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_recla) <= 1)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_imp) <= 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : Pas plus de 2 impayés sur une période de 4 semaines\n",
    "#              Au moins 1 fois des impayés sur une période de 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "    number_working_days = sum([int(not (e, d) in conges) for d in days])\n",
    "    bools_imp_whole_period = []\n",
    "    for d in days:\n",
    "        b_imp = model.NewBoolVar(f'imp_e{e}_d{d}')\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] == ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp)\n",
    "        model.Add(assignments[(e, d)] != ACT_IMP).OnlyEnforceIf(b_imp.Not())\n",
    "        bools_imp_whole_period.append(b_imp)\n",
    "    if number_working_days >= 10:\n",
    "        model.Add(sum(bools_imp_whole_period) >= 1)\n",
    "    model.Add(sum(bools_imp_whole_period) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contrainte : Pas d'impayés 2 semaines de suite\n",
    "#              ou bien pas à moins de 7 jours ouvrés consécutifs ?\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# TODO\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : Un employé ne doit pas avoir plus de 2 vendredis en Téléphone sur 4 semaines\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "if False:\n",
    "    for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "        bools_fridays = []\n",
    "        number_fridays = 0\n",
    "        for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "            friday = 4 + 5 * w\n",
    "            if not (e, friday) in conges:\n",
    "                number_fridays += 1\n",
    "        if number_fridays >= 3:\n",
    "            for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "                friday = 4 + w * 5\n",
    "                b = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_friday_e{e}_w{w}')\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, friday)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "                model.Add(assignments[(e, friday)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "                bools_fridays.append(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(sum(bools_fridays) <= 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "# Contraintes : ou bien pas 2 vendredis consécutifs de Téléphone\n",
    "# -------------------------------\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "        var_friday = []\n",
    "        for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "            friday = 5 * w + 4\n",
    "            b = model.NewBoolVar(f'tel_friday_e{e}_w1{friday}')\n",
    "            var_friday.append(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, friday)] == ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b)\n",
    "            model.Add(assignments[(e, friday)] != ACT_TEL).OnlyEnforceIf(b.Not())\n",
    "        bools_cons_fridays = []\n",
    "        for w in range(num_weeks - 1):\n",
    "            friday1 = 5 * w + 4\n",
    "            friday2 = friday1 + 5\n",
    "            if not (e, friday1) in conges and not (e, friday2) in conges:\n",
    "                bools_cons_fridays = [var_friday[w], var_friday[w + 1]]\n",
    "                model.Add(sum(bools_cons_fridays) <= 1)\n",
    "            \n",
    "\n",
    "# To write the plannings\n",
    "wb = Workbook()\n",
    "sheet = wb.active\n",
    "sheet.title = \"Planning\"\n",
    "now = datetime.now()\n",
    "filename = f\"Results\\\\Planning_{now.year:04}-{now.month:02}-{now.day:02}_{now.hour:02}h{now.minute:02}.xlsx\"\n",
    "\n",
    "iter, counter_planning = 0, 0\n",
    "max_planning = 3\n",
    "max_iter = 2 * max_planning\n",
    "success = False\n",
    "\n",
    "while counter_planning < max_planning and iter < max_iter:\n",
    "    \n",
    "    # -------------------------------\n",
    "    # Résolution\n",
    "    # -------------------------------\n",
    "    solver = cp_model.CpSolver()\n",
    "    # solver.parameters.linearization_level = 0\n",
    "    solver.parameters.randomize_search = True\n",
    "    solver.parameters.random_seed = np.random.randint(1, 500, 1).item(0)\n",
    "    status = solver.Solve(model)\n",
    "    iter += 1\n",
    "\n",
    "    if status == cp_model.OPTIMAL or status == cp_model.FEASIBLE:\n",
    "        counter_planning += 1\n",
    "        if not success: success = True\n",
    "\n",
    "        print(\"       \" + \"     \".join(employees))\n",
    "        cur_row = 2 * (counter_planning - 1) * (num_days + num_weeks) + 1\n",
    "\n",
    "        # Header\n",
    "        sheet.cell(row = cur_row, column = 2, value = f\"Planning {counter_planning}\")\n",
    "        sheet[f\"B{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=16)\n",
    "        sheet[f\"B{cur_row}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[5], end_color=dict_colors[5], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "        sheet[f\"B{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "        sheet.merge_cells(start_row = cur_row, start_column = 2, end_row = cur_row, end_column = 2 + len(employees))\n",
    "        cur_row += 1\n",
    "        sheet.cell(row = cur_row, column = 1, value = \"Date\")\n",
    "        sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "        sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "        for column_idx, employee in enumerate(employees, start = 1):\n",
    "            sheet.cell(row = cur_row, column = column_idx + 3, value = employee)\n",
    "            sheet[f\"{chr(65 + column_idx + 2)}{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "            sheet[f\"{chr(65 + column_idx + 2)}{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "\n",
    "        cur_date = first_date\n",
    "        cur_row += 1\n",
    "\n",
    "        for w in range(num_weeks):\n",
    "            for i in range(5):\n",
    "                d = 5 * w + i\n",
    "                st = f\"{d + 1:2} → \"\n",

    "                sheet.cell(row = cur_row,  column = 2, value = dict_days[i])\n",

    "                sheet.cell(row = cur_row + 1,  column = 3, value = \"AM\")\n",
    "                sheet.merge_cells(start_row = cur_row, start_column = 1, end_row = cur_row + 1, end_column = 1)\n",
    "                sheet.merge_cells(start_row = cur_row, start_column = 2, end_row = cur_row + 1, end_column = 2)\n",
    "                sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                sheet[f\"B{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                sheet[f\"C{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                sheet[f\"C{cur_row + 1}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                sheet[f\"A{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                sheet[f\"B{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                sheet[f\"C{cur_row}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                sheet[f\"C{cur_row + 1}\"].font = Font(bold=True, size=14)\n",
    "                sheet.column_dimensions['A'].width = len(str(\"--------------\"))\n",
    "                sheet.column_dimensions['B'].width = len(str(\"--------------\"))\n",
    "                sheet.row_dimensions[cur_row].height = 14\n",
    "                sheet.row_dimensions[cur_row + 1].height = 14\n",
    "                cur_date += timedelta(days = 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "                for e in range(num_employees):\n",
    "                    if not (e, d) in conges:\n",
    "                        for a in range(len(activities)):\n",
    "                            if solver.Value(assignments[(e, d)]) == a:\n",
    "                                st += f\"{activities[a]:5} \"\n",
    "                                sheet.cell(row = cur_row,  column = e + 4, value = activities[a])\n",
    "                                sheet.cell(row = cur_row + 1,  column = e + 4, value = activities[a])\n",
    "                                sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[a], end_color=dict_colors[a], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "                                sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row + 1}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[a], end_color=dict_colors[a], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "                                sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                                sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row + 1}\"].alignment = Alignment(horizontal='center', vertical='center')\n",
    "                    else:\n",
    "                        st += \"  *   \"\n",
    "                        sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[-1], end_color=dict_colors[-1], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
    "                        sheet[f\"{chr(68 + e)}{cur_row + 1}\"].fill = PatternFill(start_color=dict_colors[-1], end_color=dict_colors[-1], fill_type=\"solid\")\n",
